Welcome to the Leaf Essentials Docs

Welcome to the Docs!

This website will tell you all there is to know about Leaf Essentials.

Download Leaf Essent= ials

The current features in Leaf Essentials are:

Sidebar= =E2=80=8B

Customize your server and add scores for your players and shit

UI Build= er=E2=80=8B

Create a custom menu and let your players do stuff on it

Clans=E2=80=8B=

You can let players go in clan chat and talk about war, and the clan own= er can set a Clan Base anyone can go to! You can also configure the Clans t= o be paid!

Pre-ma= de UIs=E2=80=8B

We have UIs like Player Shops, Pay UI + more! You can open them with /scriptevent leafgui:<ui id>

Binding= =E2=80=8B

Bind any item to a UI or command. Great for server menus!
